//passenger details information Which shows on the table
class PassengerDetailsForm extends React.Component {
  render() {
    let { passengerDetails, checkForZero, transferDetails } = this.props;
    let { firstname, lastname, email, phone } = passengerDetails;
    let { passengersNumber, specialRequests } = transferDetails
    // passengerDetails, transferDetails ve icons prop'larınızdan geldiğini varsayalım.

    const detailsData = [
      {
        id: 'mainPassenger',
        icon: icons.user,
        label: 'Main Passenger',
        value: `${firstname} ${lastname}`,
        condition: true
      },
      {
        id: 'email',
        icon: icons.at,
        label: 'Email Address',
        value: email,
        condition: true
      },
      {
        id: 'phone',
        icon: icons.phone,
        label: 'Phone Number',
        value: phone,
        condition: true,
        iconClass: 'icon-circle-phone'
      },
      {
        id: 'passengers',
        icon: icons.users,
        label: 'Number of Passengers',
        value: passengersNumber,
        condition: true,
        iconClass: 'icon-circle-phone'
      },
      {
        id: 'specialRequests',
        icon: icons.notes,
        label: 'Special Requests:',
        value: specialRequests,
        condition: specialRequests && specialRequests.trim().length > 0,
        iconClass: 'icon-circle-phone'
      }
    ];
    const gapStyle = specialRequests && specialRequests.length > 0 ? "0.5rem" : "1rem";
    return (
      <div >
        <div className="contact-info-card">
          <div className="card-header contact-header">
            <h3 className="card-title">Contact Info</h3>
            {checkForZero ? "" :
              <button className="edit-button" onClick={() => this.props.onEdit()} >
                <img src={icons.edit} alt="" />
                <span>Edit</span>
              </button>
            }
          </div>

          <div className="contact-details-list" style={{ gap: gapStyle }}>
            {detailsData.map((item) => (
              <PassengerDetailRow key={item.id} id={item.id} icon={item.icon} label={item.label} value={item.value} iconClass={item.iconClass} />
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
}
//pasenger detils onchange handler form
class PassengerDetailsUpdateForm extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = {
      loading: false,
      email: this.props.passengerDetails.email,
      phone: this.props.passengerDetails.phone,
      firstname: this.props.passengerDetails.firstname,
      passengersNumber: this.props.transferDetails.passengersNumber,
      specialRequests: this.props.transferDetails.specialRequests || '',
      firstnameError: '',
      emailError: '',
      phoneError: '',
    };
  }
  onCancel() {
    if (typeof this.props.onCancel === "function") this.props.onCancel();
  }
  validateFields() {
    const { firstname, email, phone } = this.state;
    let isValid = true;
    let errors = { firstnameError: '', emailError: '', phoneError: '', };

    // 1. Ad Soyad Kontrolü
    if (!firstname) {
      errors.firstnameError = "Required";
      isValid = false;
    }

    // 2. E-posta Kontrolü
    if (!email) {
      errors.emailError = "Required";
      isValid = false;
    }
    else if (!/^\S+@\S+\.\S+$/.test(email)) {
      errors.emailError = "Please enter a valid email address.";
      isValid = false;
    }

    // 3. Telefon Kontrolü
    if (!phone) {
      errors.phoneError = "Required";
      isValid = false;
    }
    this.setState(errors);


    return isValid;
  }
  onSave() {
    if (!this.validateFields()) return;
    let { passengerDetails, transferDetails } = this.props;
    let { email, firstname, phone, passengersNumber, specialRequests } = this.state;
    let isUpdated = false;
    if (
      passengerDetails.email !== email ||
      passengerDetails.firstname !== firstname ||
      passengerDetails.phone !== phone ||
      parseInt(transferDetails.passengersNumber) !== parseInt(passengersNumber) ||
      transferDetails.specialRequests !== specialRequests
    ) {
      isUpdated = true;
    }
    if (isUpdated) {
      passengerDetails = { ...passengerDetails, email, firstname, phone };
      transferDetails = { ...transferDetails, 'passengersNumber': parseInt(passengersNumber), 'specialRequests': specialRequests };
      let params = { passengerDetails, transferDetails };
      this.setState({ loading: true }, () => {
        window.manageBookingDispatch.saveNewPassengerDetails(params, (log) => {
          if (log.status === 200) {
            this.setState({ loading: false }, () => {
              this.props.onSave();
            });
          } else {
            this.setState({ loading: false })
          }
        });
      });
    } else {
      this.props.onSave();
    }
  }

  onchangeHandler(e) {
    let { name, value } = e.target;
    if (value.includes('"') || value.includes(`'`) || value.includes('/') || value.includes('\\')) return
    this.setState({ [name]: value });
  }

  render() {
    let { loading, firstnameError, emailError, phoneError } = this.state;
    return (
      <div className="editable-psg-details">
        <div className="editable-psg-header">
          <h3 className="editable-header-title">Contact Info</h3>
          <div className="editable-buttons">
            {/* İptal Butonu */}
            <button onClick={() => this.onCancel()} className="cancel-button" disabled={loading}  >
              Close
            </button>
            {/* Kaydet Butonu */}
            <button onClick={loading ? () => { } : () => this.onSave()} className={`save-button ${loading ? 'loading' : ''}`} disabled={loading}  >
              {loading ? "loading..." : "Save"}
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>


        <div className="editable-inp-boxes">
          {/* Ad Soyad */}
          <EditableInput
            value={this.state.firstname}
            iconName="user"
            name="firstname"
            type="text"
            errorMessage={firstnameError}
            onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandler(e)}
            title="Full Name"
            placeholder="Full Name"
            icon={icons.user}
          />
          {/* E-posta */}
          <EditableInput
            value={this.state.email}
            iconName="at"
            name="email"
            type="email"
            errorMessage={emailError}
            onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandler(e)}
            icon={icons.at}
            title="Email"
            placeholder="Email"
            widthOfIcon="12px"

          />
        </div>

        <div className="editable-inp-boxes">
          {/* Yolcu Sayısı */}
          <EditableSelectBox
            value={this.state.passengersNumber}
            iconName="users"
            icon={icons.users}
            name="passengersNumber"
            onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandler(e)}
            title="Number of passengers"
            data={this.props.maxPax}
            defaultValue={this.state.passengersNumber}
            widthOfIcon="14px"

          />
          {/* Telefon Numarası */}
          <EditableInput
            value={this.state.phone}
            iconName="phone"
            name="phone"
            icon={icons.phone}
            type="tel"
            errorMessage={phoneError}
            onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandler(e)}
            title="Phone Number"
            placeholder="Phone Number"
            widthOfIcon="11px"
          />
        </div>

        <div className="editable-inp-boxes">
          <EditableTextArea
            value={this.state.specialRequests || ''}
            name="specialRequests"
            onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandler(e)}
            title="Special Requests"
            icon={false}
            placeholder="Special Requests"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
}



//journey details information  Which shows on the table
// This can optionally be placed inside a separate file: JourneyPoint.js
class JourneyPoint extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = {
      flightStatusValue: 'Loading...',
      flightStatusColor: null,
      flightData: null,
    };
  }
  // Unix zaman damgasını (timestamp), belirtilen zaman dilimine göre saat formatına çevirir
  formatTimestampToTimezone = (timestamp, timezone) => {
    if (!timestamp || !timezone) {
      return null;
    }
    // Timestamp milisaniye cinsindendir, Moment'a verilir ve belirtilen timezone'a göre formatlanır (HH:mm)
    return moment.utc(timestamp).tz(timezone).format('HH:mm');
  }
  componentDidMount() {
    const { reservationId, point } = this.props;
    const isFlightPoint = point && point.pcatId === 1;

    // Sadece bir uçuş noktası (pcatId === 1) ise API isteği yap
    if (isFlightPoint && reservationId) {
      this.fetchFlightStatus(reservationId);
    }
  }

  async fetchFlightStatus(reservationId = 940876) {
    const apiUrl = `https://api-backup.london-tech.com/api/v1/reservation/flight-status/940876?json=true`;

    try {
      const response = await fetch(apiUrl);
      console.log({ response });

      if (!response.ok) {
        if (response.status === 404) {
          this.setState({ flightStatusValue: 'Unknown', flightStatusColor: null });
        } else {
          this.setState({ flightStatusValue: `Error: ${response.status}`, flightStatusColor: null });
        }
        return;
      }
      const data = await response.json();
      console.log({ data });
      const details = data.details || {};
      const flightStatusId = details.flightStatus;
      const statusDetail = data.flightStatuses[flightStatusId] || { value: 'N/A', color: null };
      this.setState({
        flightStatusValue: statusDetail.value || 'N/A',
        flightStatusColor: statusDetail.color || null,
        flightData: details, // Tüm detayları state'e kaydet
      });

    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Uçuş durumu çekilirken bir hata oluştu:", error);
      this.setState({ flightStatusValue: ' Unknown', flightStatusColor: null, flightData: null });
    }
  }

  render() {
    const { point, type, transferDetails, } = this.props; // 'point' is the location item, 'type' indicates whether it is 'pickup' or 'dropoff'.
    const { flightStatusValue, flightStatusColor, flightData } = this.state;
    if (!point || !point.address) {
      return null;
    }





    // Check if pcatId === 1 (Flight)
    const isFlightPoint = point.pcatId === 1;
    const flightNumber = isFlightPoint ? (point.flightDetails && point.flightDetails.flightNumber) : null;
    let landingTime = transferDetails.transferDateTimeString.split(" ")[1];



    // Special icon and styling for pickups
    const isPickup = type === 'pickup';
    const iconSrc = isPickup ? icons.pickpArrowLeft : icons.mapLocationLight;
    const wrapperClass = isPickup ? "journey-card_icon-blue" : "journey-card_icon-amber";
    const pointClass = !isPickup ? "journey-card_dropoff-point" : "";
    const waitingTime = isFlightPoint ? `${point.flightDetails.waitingPickupTime}` : null

    // Durum rengini uygulamak için stil nesnesi
    const statusStyle = flightStatusColor ? { color: `#${flightStatusColor}` } : { color: `red` };




    // Display alternative details instead of address (Postcode, Cruise, Train)
    let extraDetail = "";
    if (!isFlightPoint) {
      if (point.pcatId === 5 && point.postCodeDetails) {
        extraDetail = `Postcode Address: ${point.postCodeDetails.postCodeAddress}`;
      } else if (point.pcatId === 2 && point.cruiseNumber) {
        extraDetail = `Cruise Name: ${point.cruiseNumber}`;
      } else if (point.pcatId === 3 && point.trainNumber) {
        extraDetail = `Train Number: ${point.trainNumber}`;
      } else if (point.pcatId === 7 && point["address-description"]) {
        extraDetail = `Place of Interest : ${point["address-description"]}`;
      } else if (point.pcatId === 8 && point["address-description"]) {
        extraDetail = `City Name: ${point["address-description"]}`;
      } else if (point.pcatId === 9 && point["address-description"]) {
        extraDetail = `University Name: ${point["address-description"]}`;
      } else if (point.pcatId === 10 && point["address-description"]) {
        extraDetail = `Description: ${point["address-description"]}`;
      }
      // You can add additional pcatId types here (7, 8, 9, 10)
    }



    // Sadece uçuş noktaları için gerekli verileri çıkar
    let scheduledArrival = null;
    let estimatedArrival = null;
    let actualArrival = null; // Landed durumu için kullanılabilir
    let timezone = null;
    let flightStatusId = null;

    if (isFlightPoint && flightData) {
      flightStatusId = flightData.flightStatus;
      timezone = flightData.arrivalCountry ? flightData.arrivalCountry.timezone : null;

      // Çevrilecek zaman damgalarını al
      scheduledArrival = flightData.scheduledGateArrival;
      estimatedArrival = flightData.estimatedGateArrival;
      actualArrival = flightData.actualGateArrival;
    }

    // Zaman damgalarını yerel zamana çevir
    const formattedScheduledTime = this.formatTimestampToTimezone(scheduledArrival, timezone);
    const formattedEstimatedTime = this.formatTimestampToTimezone(estimatedArrival, timezone);
    const formattedActualTime = this.formatTimestampToTimezone(actualArrival, timezone);

    // Görüntülenecek varış saatini belirle: Landed ise Actual, Estimated ise Estimated, yoksa Scheduled
    let displayArrivalTimeLabel = 'Scheduled';
    let displayArrivalTime = formattedScheduledTime;

    // Duruma göre saati güncelle (Önce Landed/Actual kontrolü yapılır)
    if (flightStatusId === 5 && formattedActualTime) { // Landed
      displayArrivalTimeLabel = 'Actual Arrival';
      displayArrivalTime = formattedActualTime;
    } else if (flightStatusId === 1 && formattedEstimatedTime) { // Estimated
      displayArrivalTimeLabel = 'Estimated Arrival';
      displayArrivalTime = formattedEstimatedTime;
    } else if (flightStatusId === 8 && formattedScheduledTime) { // Scheduled ise Scheduled kalır
      displayArrivalTimeLabel = 'Scheduled Arrival';
      displayArrivalTime = formattedScheduledTime;
    }

    return (
      <div className={`journey-card_timeline-point ${pointClass}`}>
        <div className={`journey-card_icon-wrapper ${wrapperClass}`}>
          <img src={iconSrc} alt="" />
        </div>
        <div className="journey-card_details-block">
          <p className="journey-card_location-label">{isPickup ? "Pickup" : "Drop-off"}</p>
          <p className="journey-card_location-main">{point.address}</p>

          {/* ONLY show time information if it is a pickup AND pcatId === 1 (flight) */}
          {isPickup && isFlightPoint && (
            <div className="journey-card_time-info-box">
              {/* <div className="journey-card_time-detail">
                <span className="journey-card_time-label">Scheduled:</span>
                <span className="journey-card_time-mono">{landingTime}</span>
              </div> */}
              {/* Ana Varış Saati (Scheduled, Estimated veya Actual) */}
              {displayArrivalTime && (
                <div className="journey-card_time-detail">
                  {/* Etiketi dinamik gösteriyoruz */}
                  <span className="journey-card_time-label">{displayArrivalTimeLabel}:</span>
                  <span className="journey-card_time-mono">{displayArrivalTime}</span>
                </div>
              )}
              <div className="journey-card_time-detail">
                <span className="journey-card_time-label">Flight Status:</span>
                <span className="journey-card_time-mono" style={statusStyle}>{flightStatusValue}</span>
              </div>
              {waitingTime && (
                <div className="journey-card_time-detail journey-card_time-highlight">
                  <span className="journey-card_time-label">Pickup:</span>
                  <span className="journey-card_time-mono journey-card_time-bold"> {`${landingTime} +  ${waitingTime} minutes after`}</span>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* ONLY show flight number if pcatId === 1 */}
          {isPickup && isFlightPoint && (
            <p className="journey-card_flight-tag"> Flight Number: {flightNumber}</p>
          )}
          {!isPickup && isFlightPoint && flightNumber && (<p className="journey-card_flight-tag">Flight: {flightNumber}</p>)}
          {/* Extra details for other point types */}
          {extraDetail && (
            <p className="journey-card_address">{extraDetail}</p>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

class JourneyDetailsDisplayedForm extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
  }



  render() {
    let { reservationId, transferDetails, paymentDetails, editDisabled, formattedDateFull, totalPriceWithSymbol, selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints } = this.props;
    let { paymentType } = paymentDetails;

    // Ödeme Tipi Hesaplaması (Aynı kalır)
    let paymentTypeTitle = 'Paid By Card'; // 2,5,6,7
    if (paymentType === 1) { paymentTypeTitle = 'Pay Cash to Driver' }
    if (paymentType === 4) { paymentTypeTitle = 'Account' }
    if (paymentType === 5) { paymentTypeTitle = 'Paid By PayPal' }
    let hasCashCardPayment = parseFloat(paymentDetails.byCash) && parseFloat(paymentDetails.byCash) > 0 && parseFloat(paymentDetails.byCard) && parseFloat(paymentDetails.byCard) > 0;
    if (hasCashCardPayment) { // 3
      paymentTypeTitle = 'Cash/Card'
    }

    // *** YENİ KISIM: PICKUP ve DROP-OFF VERİLERİNİ ÇEKME ***
    const pickupPoint = selectedPickupPoints[0] || {};
    const dropoffPoint = selectedDropoffPoints[0] || {};

    const JourneyTtile = () => {
      return (
        <div className="journey-card_header-wrapper">
          <h2 className="journey-card_header-title">
            <img src={icons.mapLocationLight} alt="" />
            Journey
          </h2>
          {this.props.checkFor24 || editDisabled === true ? "" :
            <button onClick={() => this.props.onEdit()} className="edit-button">
              <img src={icons.edit} alt="" />
              <span>Edit</span>
            </button>}
        </div>
      )
    }

    const JourneyFooter = () => {
      return (
        <div className="journey-card_footer-wrapper">
          <div className="journey-card_footer-date">
            <img src={icons.clock} alt="" />
            <span>{formattedDateFull}</span>
          </div>
          <div className="journey-card_footer-price-info">
            <div className="journey-card_price-main">
              {totalPriceWithSymbol}
            </div>
            <div className="journey-card_price-vat">{totalPriceWithSymbol} </div>
            <div className="journey-card_payment-method">{paymentTypeTitle}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )
    }

    return (
      <div className="journey-card_container">
        <JourneyTtile />
        <div className="journey-card_timeline-content">
          <div className="journey-card_timeline-line"></div>
          <JourneyPoint point={pickupPoint} type="pickup" transferDetails={transferDetails} reservationId={reservationId} />
          <JourneyPoint point={dropoffPoint} type="dropoff" transferDetails={transferDetails} reservationId={reservationId} />
        </div>
        <JourneyFooter />
      </div>
    );
  }
}
class JorneyDetailsUpdateForm extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = {
      quotations: [],
      pickUpPointInput: "", //in order to handleInput
      dropOffPointInput: "",
      updatedLoading: false,//when we fetch request in order to update
      pickUpSuggestions: [],
      dropOffSuggestions: [],
      quotationLoading: false,
      inputPickUpShowStatus: false, //adding input if true
      addExtraPointTextPickUp: true, //removing text if false
      inputDropOffShowStatus: false,
      addExtraPointTextDropOff: true,
      getPickUpSuggestLoading: false,
      getDropOffSuggestLoading: false,
      quotation: this.props.quotation,
      passengerEmail: this.props.email,
      payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: false,
      stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "",
      paymentType: this.props.paymentType,
      paymentToken: this.props.paymentToken,
      currentPrice: this.props.previousPrice,//it is the current price which when quotation will change it will change
      previousPrice: this.props.previousPrice,
      specialRequests: this.props.specialRequests,
      itIsCashPaymentAndChangeEfectToThePrice: false,
      transferDateTimeString: this.props.transferDateTimeString,
      hour: this.props.transferDateTimeString.split(" ")[1].split(":")[0],
      minute: this.props.transferDateTimeString.split(" ")[1].split(":")[1],
      //
      reservation: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.props.reservation)),
      persistedCountryId: null,      // incase if we delete pick up dropp both at once we need to save country id always to not crash website and get proper sggestions
    };
    this.stripeContainerRef = React.createRef();
  }
  onCancel() {
    if (typeof this.props.onCancel === "function") {
      this.props.onCancel()
      // check-point
      // window.manageBookingDispatch.onCancelJourneyDetails(JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("reservation")))
    }
  }

  //!case 1 => wetherEffectedPriceButSTillDoesntChangeTheMethod
  //*=>also it means updated already happened so we dont check isUpdated
  wetherEffectedPriceButSTillDoesntChangeTheMethod() {
    let { 'reservation': propsReservation } = this.props;
    let { 'reservation': stateReservation } = this.state;
    //
    if (JSON.stringify(propsReservation) !== JSON.stringify(stateReservation)) {
      this.setState({ updatedLoading: true }, () => {
        window.manageBookingDispatch.saveStillWantsToDoesntChangePayment({ 'reservation': stateReservation }, log => {
          if (log.status === 200) {
            this.setState({ updatedLoading: false }, () => {
              this.props.onSave();
            })
          } else {
            this.setState({ updatedLoading: false })
          }
        });
      });
    } else {
      this.props.onSave();
    }
  }

  //!case 2 he/she edited journeydetails and wants to finish payment with cash
  //*=> (will trigger componentDidUpdate to check statusof payment)
  itisCashAndWantsToPayByStripeCard(paymentType) {
    try {
      let { stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash, reservation } = this.state
      window.manageBookingDispatch.validatingTheReservationObject({ reservation }, (log) => {
        if (log.status === 200) {
          if (!stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash) {
            this.setState({ payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: true }, () => {
              let body = JSON.stringify({ 'quotations': [reservation.quotation], 'type': paymentType, language: "en", 'passengerEmail': reservation.passengerDetails.email, 'mode': localStorage['payment-mode'] || undefined, 'reservationsIds': [reservation.reservationDetails.id] })
              fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/payment/stripe/create`, { 'method': 'POST', 'headers': { "Content-Type": "application/json" }, body })
                .then((res) => res.json())
                .then(async (data) => {
                  if (data.status === 200) {
                    let scriptjs = await fetchStripePayemntScriptJs();
                    this.setState({ payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: false, stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: { ...data, scriptjs } }, () => {
                      this.checkPaymentStatus(data);
                    })
                  } else {
                    this.setState({ payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: false, stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "" })
                    window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Request Error Try contact with us")
                  }
                })
                .catch((error) => {
                  console.log(error.message);
                });
            })
          }
        } else {
          if (typeof log.error === 'object' && Array.isArray(log.error.global)) {
            window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage('', log.error.global.filter(s => typeof s === 'string').join('\n'))
            setTimeout(() => {
              let errorElements = document.querySelectorAll('.editable-error-input');
              if (errorElements && errorElements[0] && errorElements[0].offsetParent && errorElements[0].offsetParent.offsetParent) {
                errorElements[0].offsetParent.offsetParent.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
              }
            }, 1000)
          }
        }
      })
    } catch (error) {
      console.log(error);
    }
  }

  scrollToBottom() {
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (this.stripeContainerRef.current) {
        this.stripeContainerRef.current.scrollIntoView({
          behavior: "smooth",
          block: "end" // Elementi ekranın mərkəzinə gətir
        });
      }
    }, 100);
  }
  //!case 3 Subcharge
  //*=> (will trigger componentDidUpdate to check statusof payment)
  //* we dont compare if is updated or not cause alredy price changed
  paySubChargeWithStripe(paymentType) {
    let { reservation } = this.state
    try {
      window.manageBookingDispatch.validatingTheReservationObject({ reservation }, (log) => {
        if (log.status === 200) {
          let body = JSON.stringify({ 'oldQuotation': [this.props.reservation.quotation], 'newQuotation': [reservation.quotation], 'type': paymentType, 'paymentToken': reservation.paymentDetails.token, 'reservationsIds': [reservation.reservationDetails.id], 'email': reservation.passengerDetails.email, 'sessionTypeId': 2 })
          fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/payment/stripe/charges`, { 'method': 'POST', 'headers': { "Content-Type": "application/json" }, body })
            .then((res) => res.json())
            .then(async (data) => {
              if (data.status === 200) {
                let scriptjs = await fetchStripePayemntScriptJs()
                this.setState({ payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: false, stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: { ...data, scriptjs } }, () => {
                  this.checkPaymentStatus(data)
                })
                this.scrollToBottom()
              } else {
                this.setState({ payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: false, stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "" })
                window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Request Error Try contact with us ")
              }
            })
            .catch((error) => {
              console.log(error.message);
            });
        } else {
          if (typeof log.error === 'object' && Array.isArray(log.error.global)) {
            window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage('', log.error.global.filter(s => typeof s === 'string').join('\n'))
            setTimeout(() => {
              let errorElements = document.querySelectorAll('.editable-error-input');
              if (errorElements && errorElements[0] && errorElements[0].offsetParent && errorElements[0].offsetParent.offsetParent) {
                errorElements[0].offsetParent.offsetParent.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
              }
            }, 1000)
          }
        }
      })
    } catch (error) { console.log(error.message); }
  }
  // done
  addExtraInputForJourney(e, pickOrDrop) {
    if (pickOrDrop === 0) {
      this.setState({ addExtraPointTextPickUp: false, inputPickUpShowStatus: true, });
    } else {
      this.setState({ addExtraPointTextDropOff: false, inputDropOffShowStatus: true, });
    }
  }
  // Done
  fetchSuggestions(inpValue, index) {
    this.setState({ [index === 0 ? 'getPickUpSuggestLoading' : 'getDropOffSuggestLoading']: true },
      () => {
        fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/suggestions`, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify({ value: inpValue, "session-token": this.state.reservation.passengerDetails.sessionId || '', }),
        }).then((res) => res.json())
          .then((data) => {
            this.setState({
              [index === 0 ? 'dropOffSuggestions' : 'pickUpSuggestions']: [],
              getPickUpSuggestLoading: false,
              getDropOffSuggestLoading: false,
              [index === 0 ? 'pickUpSuggestions' : 'dropOffSuggestions']: [data.result],
            })
          })
          .catch((error) => {
            console.log(error)
            this.setState({ getDropOffSuggestLoading: false, getPickUpSuggestLoading: false })
          });
      })
  }
  //lhr => suggestion comes
  //Done
  onchangeHandlerGetSuggestion(e) {
    let inpName = e.target.name
    let inpValue = e.target.value
    if (inpValue.includes('"') || inpValue.includes(`'`) || inpValue.includes('/') || inpValue.includes('\\')) return
    this.setState({ [inpName]: inpValue })

    if (inpValue.length < 3) this.setState({ dropOffSuggestions: [], pickUpSuggestions: [] })

    if (inpValue.length > 2) {
      if (inpName === 'pickUpPointInput') {
        this.fetchSuggestions(inpValue, 0)
      } else {
        this.fetchSuggestions(inpValue, 1)
      }
    }
  }
  // Done
  onChangeDateSpecialRequest(e) {
    //date picker =>  {/* //2022-12-29 */ }
    let { name, value } = e.target;
    if (value.includes('"') || value.includes(`'`) || value.includes('/') || value.includes('\\')) return

    let { selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints, 'transferDetails': { transferDateTimeString } } = this.state.reservation
    if (name === "transferDateTimeString") {
      let minute = transferDateTimeString.split(" ")[1].split(":")[1]; //00   15 20 25
      let hour = transferDateTimeString.split(" ")[1].split(":")[0]; //1 2 3 4 5 6
      transferDateTimeString = `${value} ${hour}:${minute}`
      this.getQuotations({ selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints, transferDateTimeString })
      // 
      let newReservation = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.state.reservation));
      newReservation.transferDetails.transferDateTimeString = transferDateTimeString
      this.setState({ transferDateTimeString, 'reservation': newReservation })
    } else {
      let newReservation = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.state.reservation));
      newReservation.transferDetails[name] = value
      this.setState({ [name]: value, 'reservation': newReservation });
    }
  }
  //has sended to timePicker comp as a props
  // Done
  setHourOrMinute = (e, name) => {
    let value = e.target.innerText
    let { 'transferDetails': { 'transferDateTimeString': _tdts } } = this.state.reservation;
    let date = _tdts.split(" ")[0]; //2022-04-18
    let minute = _tdts.split(" ")[1].split(":")[1]; //00   15 20 25
    let hour = _tdts.split(" ")[1].split(":")[0]; //1 2 3 4 5 6
    _tdts = name === 'hour' ? `${date} ${value}:${minute}` : `${date} ${hour}:${value}`
    //
    let newReservation = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.state.reservation))
    newReservation.transferDetails.transferDateTimeString = _tdts;
    this.setState({ [name === 'hour' ? 'hour' : 'minute']: value, 'transferDateTimeString': _tdts, 'reservation': newReservation })
    this.getQuotations({ 'transferDateTimeString': _tdts })
  }
  // Done
  //!Step2 addItem to the list
  addItemToListPart2(point, index, type) {
    let { reservation } = this.state;
    let newReservation = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(reservation))
    if (index === 0) {
      newReservation.selectedPickupPoints.push(point)
    };
    if (index === 1) {
      newReservation.selectedDropoffPoints.push(point)
    };
    //update automatically quotation
    let { 'transferDetails': { transferDateTimeString } } = newReservation;
    let params = { 'selectedPickupPoints': newReservation.selectedPickupPoints, 'selectedDropoffPoints': newReservation.selectedDropoffPoints, transferDateTimeString }
    this.getQuotations(params)
    this.setState({ 'reservation': newReservation });

  }
  // has sended to handleSearch comp as a props //!Step1 addItem to the list
  // done
  handleAddItemToSelectList = (item, objDetails, index, type) => {
    let method = "POST"
    let headers = { "Content-Type": "application/json", }
    //
    if (item.ptype === 3) { // for google points only
      let body = JSON.stringify({ point: item });
      //request for google place and add item to the list
      fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/google-places`, { method, headers, body })
        .then((res) => res.json())
        .then((data) => {
          if (data.status === 200) {
            let point = { ...objDetails, ...data.point };
            this.removeAddInputField(index, () => {
              this.addItemToListPart2(point, index, type)
            })
          }
        })
        .catch((error) => {
          console.log(error);
        });
    } else if (item.pcatId === 5) { // for postcode points 
      let body = JSON.stringify({ postcodes: [item.postcode] })
      //request forpost codes
      fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/postcode-address`, { method, headers, body })
        .then((res) => res.json())
        .then((data) => {
          if (data.status) window.reaervationDetailsDispatch.setSelectedPostCode(data.results[0]);
        })
        .catch((error) => {
          console.log(error);
        });
      let point = { ...item, ...objDetails };
      this.removeAddInputField(index, () => {
        this.addItemToListPart2(point, index, type)
      })
    } else { // for rest points
      let point = { ...item, ...objDetails };
      this.removeAddInputField(index, () => {
        this.addItemToListPart2(point, index, type)
      })
    }
  }
  // Done
  deleteItemFromList = (pickOrDropPoint, indexOfCurrentItem) => {
    let { reservation } = this.state;
    //
    let newReservation = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(reservation))
    let targetPointsKey = `selected${pickOrDropPoint === 0 ? 'Pickup' : 'Dropoff'}Points`;
    newReservation[targetPointsKey] = newReservation[targetPointsKey].filter((point, i) => i !== indexOfCurrentItem)

    this.setState({ 'reservation': newReservation }, () => {
      this.getQuotations({ 'selectedPickupPoints': newReservation.selectedPickupPoints || [], 'selectedDropoffPoints': newReservation.selectedDropoffPoints || [] })
    })
    //update automatically quotation
  }
  // Done
  selectQuotation = (item) => {
    let newReservation = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.state.reservation));
    newReservation['quotation'] = item
    if (newReservation.paymentDetails.paymentType === 1) {
      newReservation.paymentDetails.price = parseFloat(item.price);
    }
    // check pax number
    if (Array.isArray(window.carsTypes)) {
      let { pax = 1 } = carsTypes.find(obj => obj.id === item.carId) || {}
      if (pax < newReservation.transferDetails.passengersNumber) {
        newReservation.transferDetails.passengersNumber = pax
      }
    }
    this.setState({ quotation: item, currentPrice: item.price, 'reservation': newReservation })
  }
  // Done
  getQuotations(params = {}) {
    let { reservation } = this.state;
    let { selectedPickupPoints = reservation.selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints = reservation.selectedDropoffPoints, transferDateTimeString = reservation.transferDetails.transferDateTimeString, paymentDetails = reservation.paymentDetails } = params
    //so we use here country id which we saved in state
    let countryId = this.state.persistedCountryId;
    this.setState({ quotationLoading: true }, () => {
      let body = JSON.stringify({ selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints, transferDateTimeString, 'currencyId': paymentDetails.currencyId, 'countryId': countryId, 'account': 1, 'configurations': { ignoreDisabledSalesDays: true } });
      fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/quotation`, { 'method': 'POST', 'headers': { "Content-Type": "application/json" }, body })
        .then((res) => res.json()).then((data) => {
          if (data.status === 200) {
            let selectedQuotaion = data.quotationOptions.filter((quotation) => quotation.carId === this.state.quotation.carId || this.state.reservation.quotation.carId === quotation.carId)[0]
            if (typeof selectedQuotaion === 'object') {
              this.setState({ quotations: data.quotationOptions }, () => {
                let originQuotation = reservation.quotation || {};
                if (originQuotation.carId === selectedQuotaion.carId) {
                  if (parseFloat(selectedQuotaion.price) > parseFloat(originQuotation.price)) {
                    this.selectQuotation(selectedQuotaion)
                  }
                } else {
                  this.selectQuotation(selectedQuotaion) // select the first quotation
                }
              })
            }
          } else {
            this.setState({ quotations: [] })
          }
          this.setState({ quotationLoading: false });
        })
        .catch((error) => {
          this.setState({ quotationLoading: false });
          window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", error.message);
        });
    })
  }
  // Done
  removeAddInputField(index, callback = () => { }) {
    if ([0, 1].includes(index)) {
      this.setState({
        [`${index === 1 ? 'dropOff' : 'pickUp'}PointInput`]: "",
        [`${index === 1 ? 'dropOff' : 'pickUp'}Suggestions`]: [],
        [`input${index === 1 ? 'DropOff' : 'PickUp'}ShowStatus`]: false,
        [`addExtraPointText${index === 1 ? 'DropOff' : 'PickUp'}`]: true,
      }, () => callback())
    }
  }
  componentDidMount() {
    // collect quatations details
    let { selectedDropoffPoints, selectedPickupPoints, transferDetails: { transferDateTimeString } } = this.props.reservation;
    this.getQuotations({ selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints, transferDateTimeString });
    // set global functions into journeyDetailsUpdateFormDispatch global variable
    window.journeyDetailsUpdateFormDispatch = {
      onchangeItemDetails: ((updatedValues, pickOrDrop, whichItem, pcatId) => {
        let newReservation = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.state.reservation))
        let { selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints } = newReservation
        if (pickOrDrop === 0) {
          if (pcatId === 1) {
            selectedPickupPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedPickupPoints[whichItem], flightDetails: updatedValues }
          }
          if (pcatId === 2) {
            selectedPickupPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedPickupPoints[whichItem], cruiseNumber: updatedValues }
          }
          if (pcatId === 3) {
            selectedPickupPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedPickupPoints[whichItem], trainNumber: updatedValues }
          }
          if (pcatId === 5) {
            selectedPickupPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedPickupPoints[whichItem], postCodeDetails: updatedValues }
          }
          if (pcatId === 7 || pcatId === 8 || pcatId === 9 || pcatId === 10) {
            selectedPickupPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedPickupPoints[whichItem], ["address-description"]: updatedValues }
          }
        }
        if (pickOrDrop === 1) {
          if (pcatId === 1) {
            selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem], flightDetails: updatedValues }
          }
          if (pcatId === 2) {
            selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem], cruiseNumber: updatedValues }
          }
          if (pcatId === 3) {
            selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem], trainNumber: updatedValues }
          }
          if (pcatId === 5) {
            selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem], postCodeDetails: updatedValues }
          }
          if (pcatId === 7 || pcatId === 8 || pcatId === 9 || pcatId === 10) {
            selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem] = { ...selectedDropoffPoints[whichItem], ["address-description"]: updatedValues }
          }
        }
        if ([0, 1].includes(pickOrDrop)) {
          newReservation.selectedDropoffPoints = selectedDropoffPoints;
          newReservation.selectedPickupPoints = selectedPickupPoints;
          this.setState({ selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints, 'reservation': newReservation })
        } else { console.log(`unexoected values for pickOrDrop`, { pickOrDrop }) }
      }).bind(this),
      setStripeIframeToNull: () => this.setState({ stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "" })
    }
    this.setState({
      persistedCountryId: (selectedPickupPoints || [{}])[0] ? (selectedPickupPoints || [{}])[0].countryId : null,
    })
  }

  checkPaymentStatus(paymentSessionData = {}) {
    let { webSocketToken, href } = paymentSessionData || {};
    let { reservation } = this.state;
    let interVal;
    if (webSocketToken) {
      interVal = setInterval(async () => {
        try {
          let req = await fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/payment/status`, { 'method': 'POST', 'headers': { "Content-Type": "application/json", }, 'body': JSON.stringify({ token: webSocketToken }) });
          let resp = await req.json();
          if (resp.status === 200) {
            //we r checking here in order to be sure it is stripe payment or not In future we can add more payments
            if (href.includes("stripe")) {
              window.manageBookingDispatch.setPaymentTokenAndEditReservation({ 'response': resp.data, reservation }, log => {
                if (log.status === 200) {
                  this.props.onSave()
                }
              })
            } else {
              window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Something went wrong Try contact with us")
              this.setState({ stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "" })
            }
            clearInterval(interVal);
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.log(error);
        }
      }, 2000);
    }
  }
  render() {
    let {
      objectDetailss,
      carsTypesObject,
      postCodeAddress,
      imageTypesObject,
      setModalCarStatus,
      namePlaceTypesObject,
      setModalFlightStatus,
      objectDetailStatuses,
    } = this.props;
    let {
      hour,
      minute,
      quotations,
      paymentType,
      currentPrice,
      previousPrice,
      updatedLoading,
      pickUpPointInput,
      quotationLoading,
      dropOffPointInput,
      pickUpSuggestions,
      dropOffSuggestions,
      inputPickUpShowStatus,
      inputDropOffShowStatus,
      addExtraPointTextPickUp,
      getPickUpSuggestLoading,
      getDropOffSuggestLoading,
      addExtraPointTextDropOff,
      reservation,
    } = this.state;
    let { quotation, selectedPickupPoints, selectedDropoffPoints, paymentDetails } = reservation;
    //replacing slahs with  -  24/12/2022  => change to  2022-12-24
    let date = null
    if (this.state.transferDateTimeString.includes("/")) {
      date = (this.state.transferDateTimeString
        .split(" ")[0]
        .replace(/\//g, "-")
        .split(" ")[0]
        .replace(/(\d+)\-(\d+)-(\d+)/, "$3-$2-$1"))
    } else {
      date = this.state.transferDateTimeString.split(" ")[0]
    }

    let { payStripeLoadingInCaseCash, stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash } = this.state
    let disabled = !(selectedPickupPoints.length > 0 && selectedDropoffPoints.length > 0 && (parseFloat(currentPrice) <= parseFloat(previousPrice) || paymentType === 1) && quotations.length > 0)
    const surchargeStatus = (quotations.length > 0 && (parseFloat(currentPrice) - parseFloat(previousPrice)) > 0)

    const SurhcahrgeComponent = () => {
      return (<div className="informative-subcharges-div">
        <div className="informative-subcharge-price-info ">
          <p id="informationMessage">Due to the amendments you have made;</p>
          <p id="informationMessage">New Journey price : £ {currentPrice}</p>
          <p id="informationMessage">Previous journey price : £ {`${previousPrice}.00`}</p>
          <p id="informationMessage" className="difference-price">Price difference : {(((__resources || {}).paymentCurrencies || {})[paymentDetails.currencyId] || {}).symbol || '£'} {`${+currentPrice - +previousPrice}.00`}</p>
        </div>
      </div>

      )
    }
    const PayButton = ({ visibleOndesktop = false }) => {
      if (quotations.length > 0 && paymentType === 1) {
        return <button className={`button-base pay-button ${visibleOndesktop ? "visible-on-desktop" : ""}`} onClick={() => this.itisCashAndWantsToPayByStripeCard(7)}>{payStripeLoadingInCaseCash ? "Loading.." : "Pay by Card"}</button>;
      }

      if (quotations.length > 0 && paymentType !== 1 && parseFloat(currentPrice) - parseFloat(previousPrice) > 0) {
        return (
          <button className={`button-base pay-button ${visibleOndesktop ? "visible-on-desktop" : ""}`} onClick={() => {
            this.paySubChargeWithStripe(7);
            this.scrollToBottom()
          }}>
            {payStripeLoadingInCaseCash ? "Loading.." : "Pay Surcharge by Card"}
          </button>
        );
      }

    };
    const IframeDiv = () => {
      return (
        <div className="iframe-rsv-container" style={{ marginTop: '1rem' }} ref={this.stripeContainerRef}>
          <div className="iframe-div-in-case-cash">
            <div id='aplStripeElement' style={{ maxWidth: '500px', width: '100%', zIndex: 1000 }} data={JSON.stringify(stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash)}></div>
          </div>
        </div>
      );
    };
    return (
      <div className="editable-jrn-details">
        <div className="editable-jrn-header ">
          <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", width: "100%" }}>
            <h1>Journey Details</h1>
            <div className="editable-jrn-header-actions">
              <button onClick={() => this.onCancel()} className="cancel-button">Close</button>
              <button onClick={updatedLoading ? () => { } : () => this.wetherEffectedPriceButSTillDoesntChangeTheMethod()} disabled={disabled} className={`save-button  ${disabled ? "disabled" : ""}`}  >{updatedLoading ? "Loading" : "Save"}</button>
              <PayButton visibleOndesktop={true} />
            </div>
          </div>
          {surchargeStatus ? <SurhcahrgeComponent /> : <React.Fragment></React.Fragment>}
        </div>

        <div className="editable-jrn-main-grid">
          {/* Left column deails  */}
          <div className="editable-jrn-left-column">
            <div className="editable-card">
              <div className="editable-card-header">
                <h2>Route Details</h2>
              </div>
              <div className="editable-card-body">
                {/* pick up section */}

                {selectedPickupPoints.length > 0 ?
                  <SelectedLists
                    pickOrDrop={0}
                    postCodeAddress={postCodeAddress}
                    imageTypesObject={imageTypesObject}
                    selectedItems={selectedPickupPoints}
                    setModalFlightStatus={setModalFlightStatus} //when click to info
                    objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses}
                    deleteItemFromList={this.deleteItemFromList}
                    addExtraPickStatus={addExtraPointTextPickUp}
                    addExtraPointClick={(e) => this.addExtraInputForJourney(e, 0)}
                    onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandlerGetSuggestion(e)}
                    inputValue={pickUpPointInput}
                    name="pickUpPointInput"
                    isLoading={getPickUpSuggestLoading}
                  /> : ""}

                {(selectedPickupPoints.length === 0 || inputPickUpShowStatus) &&
                  <div className="point-row" style={{ marginTop: '1rem' }}>
                    <div style={{ marginTop: '0px' }} className={`point-icon point-icon-blue-row`}>
                      <img src={icons.mapLocationLight} alt="" />
                    </div>
                    <div className="point-content" style={{ position: 'relative' }}>
                      <div className="point-header">
                        <label className="label-xs">
                          {"Pick Up Location"}
                        </label>

                      </div>
                      <input
                        name="pickUpPointInput"
                        placeholder="City or Airport"
                        type="text" value={pickUpPointInput}
                        onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandlerGetSuggestion(e)}
                        className="input-underline"
                      />

                      <HandleSearchResults
                        index={0}
                        type={"pickup"}
                        objectDetailss={objectDetailss}
                        imageTypesObject={imageTypesObject}
                        pickOrDropItems={pickUpSuggestions}
                        namePlaceTypesObject={namePlaceTypesObject}
                        handleAddItemToSelectList={this.handleAddItemToSelectList}
                      />
                      {getPickUpSuggestLoading && (
                        <div className="editable-input-loading-circle editable-input-loading-circle-blue" >
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>

                  </div>}

                {
                  selectedDropoffPoints.length > 0 ?
                    <SelectedLists
                      pickOrDrop={1}
                      postCodeAddress={postCodeAddress}
                      imageTypesObject={imageTypesObject}
                      selectedItems={selectedDropoffPoints}
                      objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses}
                      deleteItemFromList={this.deleteItemFromList}
                      addExtraPickStatus={addExtraPointTextDropOff}
                      addExtraPointClick={(e) => this.addExtraInputForJourney(e, 1)}
                      onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandlerGetSuggestion(e)}
                      name="dropOffPointInput"

                    /> : ""
                }
                {(selectedDropoffPoints.length === 0 || inputDropOffShowStatus) &&
                  <div className="point-row" style={{ marginTop: '1rem' }}>
                    <div style={{ marginTop: '0px' }} className={`point-icon point-icon-orange-row`}>
                      <img src={icons.mapLocationLight} alt="" />
                    </div>
                    <div className="point-content">
                      <div className="point-header">
                        <label className="label-xs">
                          {"Drop Off Location"}
                        </label>
                      </div>
                      <input name="dropOffPointInput" placeholder="City or Airport" type="text" value={dropOffPointInput} onChange={(e) => this.onchangeHandlerGetSuggestion(e)} className="input-underline" />
                      <HandleSearchResults
                        index={1}
                        type={"drop"}
                        objectDetailss={objectDetailss}
                        imageTypesObject={imageTypesObject}
                        pickOrDropItems={dropOffSuggestions}
                        namePlaceTypesObject={namePlaceTypesObject}
                        handleAddItemToSelectList={this.handleAddItemToSelectList}
                      />
                      {getDropOffSuggestLoading && (
                        <div className="editable-input-loading-circle editable-input-loading-circle-orange" >
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>}



              </div>

            </div>
            {/* landing time details hour datepickup */}
            <div className="editable-card">
              <div className="editable-card-header">
                <h2>Landing Details</h2>
              </div>
              <div className="editable-card-body">
                {/* dateInput timehour getQuotationBtn */}
                <div className="editable-jrn-date-hour-minute-div">
                  <div className="editable-jrn-departing-date">
                    {/* //2022-12-29 */}
                    <DateInput
                      type="date"
                      value={date}
                      name="transferDateTimeString"
                      icon={icons.calendar}
                      classNameImg="icon-inside-small-input"
                      onChange={(e) => this.onChangeDateSpecialRequest(e)}
                      title={`
               ${selectedPickupPoints.length > 0 && selectedPickupPoints[0].pcatId === 1
                          ? "Flight Landing Date"
                          : "Pick Up Date"
                        }`}
                    />
                  </div>
                  <div className="editable-jrn-detparting-time">
                    <TimePicker
                      hour={hour}
                      name="hour"
                      options={hourss}
                      setHourOrMinute={this.setHourOrMinute}
                      title={`
              ${selectedPickupPoints.length > 0 && selectedPickupPoints[0].pcatId === 1
                          ? "Landing Hour"
                          : "Pick Up Hour"
                        }`}
                    />
                    <TimePicker
                      name="minute"
                      minute={minute}
                      options={minutes}
                      setHourOrMinute={this.setHourOrMinute}
                      title={`
              ${selectedPickupPoints.length > 0 && selectedPickupPoints[0].pcatId === 1
                          ? "Landing Minute"
                          : "Pick Up Minute"
                        }`}
                    />
                  </div>

                </div>

                {/* special request  */}
                <TextArea
                  classNameImg=""
                  fromBooking={true}
                  icon={icons.idBadge}
                  name="specialRequests"
                  title="Special Requests"
                  value={this.state.specialRequests}
                  onChange={(e) => this.onChangeDateSpecialRequest(e)}
                />
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="editable-footer-button-div">
              <button className="save-button" onClick={() => this.getQuotations()}>
                Get Quotation
              </button>
            </div>
            {stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash ? (
              <IframeDiv />) : ""}

          </div>

          {/* right column details */}
          <div className="editable-jrn-right-column">
            {/* benefit box */}
            <div className="editable-card">
              <BenefitBox />
              <div className="quotes-container">
                {quotations.length > 0 ?
                  <QuotationCardItemm
                    quotation={quotation}
                    quotations={quotations}
                    carsTypesObject={carsTypesObject}
                    quotationLoading={quotationLoading}
                    setModalCarStatus={setModalCarStatus}
                    selectQuotation={item => this.selectQuotation(item)}
                  />
                  : <div style={{ postion: 'relative' }} className="quotaion-card-div-items">
                    <Loading loadCenter={true} />
                  </div>}
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="editable-jrn-header-actions visible-on-mobile-header-editable-jrn-actions ">
              <button onClick={() => this.onCancel()} className="cancel-button">Close</button>
              <PayButton />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>



      </div>
    );
  }
}

class SelectedLists extends React.Component {
  render() {
    let {
      pickOrDrop, selectedItems, postCodeAddress, imageTypesObject,
      deleteItemFromList, objectDetailStatuses, setModalFlightStatus,
      addExtraPickStatus, addExtraPointClick,
      isLoading,

    } = this.props;
    const isPickUpOrDropOff = pickOrDrop === 0
    const PickText = pickOrDrop === 1 ? "Pick Up Location" : " Drop Off Location"


    return (
      <div>
        {selectedItems.length > 0 ? selectedItems.map((item, i) => {
          return (
            <div className={`editable-card-body-section-box editable-card-body-section-${!isPickUpOrDropOff ? "dropoff" : "pickup"}`}>

              <div className="point-row">
                <div className={`point-icon point-icon-${!isPickUpOrDropOff ? 'orange' : 'blue'}-row`}>
                  <img src={icons.mapLocationLight} alt="" />
                </div>
                <div className="point-content">
                  <div className="point-header">
                    <label className="label-xs">
                      {PickText}
                    </label>
                    <button onClick={(e) => deleteItemFromList(this.props.pickOrDrop, i, item)} className="btn-remove" title="Remove">
                      <img src={icons.trash} alt="" />
                    </button>
                  </div>
                  <input type="text" value={item.address} readOnly className="input-underline" />
                </div>
              </div>


              <CheckForFlight item={item} index={pickOrDrop} whichItemSelected={i} setModalFlightStatus={setModalFlightStatus} objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses} />
              <CheckingForPostcodes item={item} index={pickOrDrop} whichItemSelected={i} postCodeAddress={postCodeAddress} objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses} />

              <CheckForCruises item={item} index={pickOrDrop} whichItemSelected={i} objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses} />
              <CheckForTrain item={item} index={pickOrDrop} whichItemSelected={i} objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses} />
              <CheckPlaceOfInterest item={item} index={pickOrDrop} whichItemSelected={i} objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses} />
              <CheckForCitites item={item} index={pickOrDrop} whichItemSelected={i} objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses} />
              <CheckForUniversity item={item} index={pickOrDrop} whichItemSelected={i} objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses} />
              <CheckForOther item={item} index={pickOrDrop} whichItemSelected={i} objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses} />

              {addExtraPickStatus && selectedItems.length !== 0 && (
                <div onClick={() => addExtraPointClick()} className="btn-add">
                  + Add Extra Dropoff Point
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          );
        }) : ""}
      </div>
    );
  }
}
