class VehicleCard extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = {
      isLuggageInfoOpen: false,
      lightboxImageUrl: null,
    };
    this.handleLuggageInfoClick = this.handleLuggageInfoClick.bind(this);
    this.openLightbox = this.openLightbox.bind(this);
    this.closeLightbox = this.closeLightbox.bind(this);
  }

  // 2. Tıklama İşleyici (Handler)
  handleLuggageInfoClick() {
    this.setState(prevState => ({
      isLuggageInfoOpen: !prevState.isLuggageInfoOpen,
    }));
  }
  // Lightbox'ı açan fonksiyon
  openLightbox(imageUrl) {
    this.setState({ lightboxImageUrl: imageUrl });
  }

  // Lightbox'ı kapatan fonksiyon
  closeLightbox() {
    this.setState({ lightboxImageUrl: null });
  }

  render() {
    const { carName, paxCount, suitcaseCount, carImage, luggageImage, luggageImage2 } = this.props;
    const { isLuggageInfoOpen, lightboxImageUrl } = this.state;
    return (
      <div className="card vehicle-card">
        <div className="card-header vehicle-card-header">
          <div>
            <h3 className="card-title">
              Vehicle Type
            </h3>
            {/* Props kullanımı: {propAdı} */}
            <p className="vehicle-name">{carName}</p>
            <p className="vehicle-capacity-text">
              Capacity: {paxCount} Pax with {suitcaseCount} Suitcases
            </p>
          </div>

          {/* Event handler (olay işleyici) props olarak kullanılıyor */}
          <button onClick={this.handleLuggageInfoClick} className={`edit-button-executive`}>
            <img src={`${!isLuggageInfoOpen ? icons.angleDown : icons.angleUp}`} alt="Info Icon" />
            <span>
              Luggage Info
            </span>
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Images Grid */}
        <div className="vehicle-image-grid">
          {/* Car Image */}
          <div className="image-wrapper vehicle-image">
            <img className="car-img" src={carImage} alt="Car" />
            <div className="image-overlay pax-badge">
              <div className="image-overlay-content">
                <img src={icons.user} alt="User Icon" />
                {paxCount}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Capacity/Luggage Image */}
          <div className={`image-wrapper luggage-image `} onClick={() => this.openLightbox(luggageImage2)}>
            <img src={luggageImage2} className="image-content luggage-capacity-img" alt="Luggage Capacity" />
            <div className=" view-badge" >
              <div className="image-overlay-content">
                <img src={icons.view} alt="View Icon" />
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="image-overlay luggage-badge">
              <div className="image-overlay-content">
                <img src={icons.suitcase} alt="Suitcase Icon" />
                {suitcaseCount}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

        </div>
        <div className={`luggage-info-container ${isLuggageInfoOpen ? 'open' : ''}`}>
          <div className="vehicle-image-grid">

            <div className={`image-wrapper vehicle-image `} onClick={() => this.openLightbox(luggageImage)}   >
              <div className="view-badge">
                <div className="image-overlay-content">
                  <img src={icons.view} alt="View Icon" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <img className="image-content luggage-capacity-img" src={luggageImage} alt="Car" />
            </div>

            <div className={`image-wrapper vehicle-image `} onClick={() => this.openLightbox(luggageImage2)}  >
              <div className=" view-badge">
                <div className="image-overlay-content">
                  <img src={icons.view} alt="View Icon" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <img
                src={luggageImage2}
                className="image-content luggage-capacity-img"
                alt="Luggage Capacity"
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        {lightboxImageUrl && (
          <div className="lightbox-overlay" onClick={this.closeLightbox}>
            <div className="lightbox-content" onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}>
              <button className="lightbox-close-button" onClick={this.closeLightbox}>
                &times;
              </button>
              <img src={lightboxImageUrl} alt="Zoomed View" className="lightbox-image" />
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  }
}
class TaxiTrackerMap extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { isMapLoading: true, };
    this.handleMapLoad = this.handleMapLoad.bind(this);
  }

  handleMapLoad() {
    this.setState({ isMapLoading: false });
  }

  render() {
    let mapUrl = `${__env.trackMyTaxiUrl}/${this.props.reservationToken}?isPassenger=true`
    const containerHeight = this.props.height || '600px';

    return (
      <div className="rsv-section-container">
        <div className="rsv-section-taxi-content" style={{ position: 'relative', height: containerHeight }}>

          {this.state.isMapLoading && (
            <div className="map-loading-overlay">
              <div className="spinner-center">
                <div className="spinner"></div>
                <p>Map is Loading...</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          <iframe
            src={mapUrl}
            title="Taxi Tracking Map"
            width="100%"
            height="100%"
            frameBorder="0"
            allowFullScreen
            scrolling="no"
            onLoad={this.handleMapLoad}
            style={{
              display: this.state.isMapLoading ? 'none' : 'block'
            }}
          >
          </iframe>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
}
class FixedActionBar extends React.Component {
  render() {
    // Extract all required props
    const {
      paymentDetails,
      totalPriceWithSymbol,
      stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash,
      reservationDetails,
      payStripeLoadingInCaseCash,
      hasCashCardPayment,
      isCashCardPaymentInProgress,
      isCashCardPaymentLoading,
      payByStripe, // Payment handler functions
      payCashCard,
      onTrackTaxiClick // Callback for the "Track Taxi" button
    } = this.props;

    // Driver is considered "en route" if driverStatusId is not 9
    const isDriverEnRoute = reservationDetails.driverStatusId !== 9;

    // Determine when the Track Taxi button should be shown
    // Track button should be shown unless the Cash-by-Card button is visible
    const shouldRenderTrackButton =
      !(hasCashCardPayment && isCashCardPaymentInProgress === false && isDriverEnRoute);

    return (
      <div className="fixed-action-bar">
        <div className="button-wrapper">

          {/* --------------------- PAYMENT BUTTON --------------------- */}
          {/* If paymentType is NOT 1 → payment is already completed */}
          {paymentDetails.paymentType !== 1 ? (
            <button className="action-button pay-button">
              <img src={icons.creditCard} alt="Credit Card" />
              {`Paid ${totalPriceWithSymbol}`}
            </button>
          ) : (
            // paymentType === 1 → unpaid or cash payment
            // Hide card payment button if Stripe iframe/token exists or driver is not en route
            (stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash || !isDriverEnRoute) ? (
              <React.Fragment></React.Fragment>
            ) : (
              <button className="action-button pay-button" onClick={() => payByStripe(7)} >
                <img src={icons.creditCard} alt="Credit Card" />
                {payStripeLoadingInCaseCash ? "Loading.." : `Pay ${totalPriceWithSymbol}`}
              </button>
            )
          )}

          {/* ----------------- PAY CASH BY CARD BUTTON ----------------- */}
          {/* This button appears only when cash can still be paid by card */}
          {(hasCashCardPayment && isCashCardPaymentInProgress === false && isDriverEnRoute) ? (
            <button onClick={payCashCard} className="button-base">
              {isCashCardPaymentLoading ? "Loading ..." : "Pay your Cash by Card"}
            </button>
          ) : (
            <React.Fragment></React.Fragment>
          )}

          {/* ------------------- TRACK TAXI BUTTON ------------------- */}
          {/* Track Taxi button should appear when Cash-by-Card button is NOT visible */}
          {shouldRenderTrackButton ? (
            <button className="action-button track-button" onClick={onTrackTaxiClick}   >
              <img src={icons.track} alt="Track Taxi" />
              Track Taxi
            </button>
          ) : (
            <div></div>
          )}

        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

class ReservationDetails extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = {
      setModalCar: false,
      setModalFlight: false,
      journeyEditStatus: false,
      passengerEditStatus: false,
      stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "",
      payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: false,
      reservation: this.props.reservation,
      checkFor24: null,
      checkForZero: null,
      postCodeAddress: [],
      isMailSending: false,
      isInvoiceMailSending: false,
      //cash card payment
      cashCardPaymentDetails: null,
      isCashCardPaymentInProgress: false,
      isCashCardPaymentLoading: false,
      activeTab: 'details',
      isLuggageInfoOpen: true,
      isMapLoading: true,
    };
    this.handleMapLoad = this.handleMapLoad.bind(this);
  }
  handleMapLoad() {
    // iframe tamamen yüklendiğinde bu fonksiyon çalışır
    this.setState({ isMapLoading: false });
  }
  //!case 0 It is cash payment and he wants to change payment directly to card
  payByStripe(type) {
    //get quotaion from state after clicking to save button
    let { stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash } = this.state
    let { reservation } = this.props;
    let { quotation, passengerDetails: { email } } = reservation
    let body = JSON.stringify({ 'quotations': [quotation], type, language: "en", passengerEmail: email, mode: localStorage['payment-mode'] || undefined, 'reservationsIds': [reservation.reservationDetails.id] })
    try {
      if (!stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash) {
        this.setState({ payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: true }, () => {
          fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/payment/stripe/create`, { 'method': 'POST', 'headers': { "Content-Type": "application/json", }, body })
            .then((res) => res.json())
            .then(async (data) => {
              if (data.status === 200) {
                let scriptjs = await fetchStripePayemntScriptJs();
                this.setState({ payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: false, stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: { ...data, scriptjs } }, () => {
                  this.checkPaymentStatus(data)
                  setTimeout(() => {
                    if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {
                      // Scrolls to the bottom of the page
                      window.scrollTo({
                        top: document.body.scrollHeight,
                        behavior: 'smooth'
                      });
                    }
                  }, 700);
                })
              } else {
                this.setState({ payStripeLoadingInCaseCash: false, stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "" })
                window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Request Error Try contact with us ")
              }
            })
            .catch((error) => { console.log(error.message); });
        })
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log(error);
    }
  }
  payCashCard() {
    //get quotaion from state after clicking to save button
    let { cashCardPaymentDetails } = this.state
    let { reservation } = this.props;
    let { passengerDetails: { email }, paymentDetails: { byCard, byCash, token }, quotation, reservationDetails } = reservation;
    let oldQuotation = [{ 'carId': quotation.carId, 'price': byCard }];
    let newQuotation = [{ 'carId': quotation.carId, 'price': byCard + byCash }];
    let body = JSON.stringify({
      oldQuotation,
      newQuotation,
      byCard,
      byCash,
      'type': 7,
      'sessionTypeId': 5,
      email,
      'mode': localStorage['payment-mode'] === 'sandbox' ? 1 : 2,
      'reservationsIds': [reservationDetails.id],
      'paymentToken': token,
    })
    try {
      if (cashCardPaymentDetails === null) {
        this.setState({ isCashCardPaymentLoading: true }, () => {
          fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/payment/stripe/charges`, { 'method': 'POST', 'headers': { "Content-Type": "application/json", }, body })
            .then((res) => res.json())
            .then(async (data) => {
              if (data.status === 200) {
                await fetchStripePayemntScriptJs({ data });
                this.setState({ isCashCardPaymentLoading: false, isCashCardPaymentInProgress: true, cashCardPaymentDetails: { ...data } }, () => {
                  this.checkPaymentStatus(data)
                })
              } else {
                this.setState({ isCashCardPaymentLoading: false, isCashCardPaymentInProgress: false, cashCardPaymentDetails: null })
                window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Request Error Try contact with us ")
              }
            }).catch((error) => {
              this.setState({ isCashCardPaymentLoading: false, isCashCardPaymentInProgress: false, cashCardPaymentDetails: null })
              window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Request Error Try contact with us ")
            });
        })
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log(error);
    }
  }
  sendBookingAsEmail(params = {}) {
    let { type = 'details' } = params;
    let { isMailSending, reservation, isInvoiceMailSending } = this.state;
    if (isMailSending === false && isInvoiceMailSending === false) {
      this.setState({ [type === 'invoice' ? 'isInvoiceMailSending' : 'isMailSending']: true }, () => {
        let { 'reservationDetails': { 'id': reservationId }, 'passengerDetails': { email } } = reservation;
        fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/reservation/${type === 'invoice' ? 'invoice' : 'mail'}/${reservationId}`, { 'method': 'GET', 'headers': { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, redirect: 'follow' })
          .then(response => response.json())
          .then(result => {
            if (result.status === 200) {
              let emailOptions = {
                'method': "POST",
                'body': JSON.stringify({
                  'senderId': 1,
                  'reciverMails': [email],
                  'subject': `Booking ${type === 'invoice' ? 'Invoice' : 'Details'} ${reservationId} Airport Pickups London`,
                  'mailContent': result.data.template,
                }),
                'headers': { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
              };
              fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/tools/mailer`, emailOptions).then(res => res.json())
                .then((res) => {
                  if (res.status === 200) {
                    window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("Email sent successfully", "")
                  } else {
                    window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Request Error Try contact with us ")
                  }
                  this.setState({ [type === 'invoice' ? 'isInvoiceMailSending' : 'isMailSending']: false })
                }).catch(error => {
                  this.setState({ [type === 'invoice' ? 'isInvoiceMailSending' : 'isMailSending']: false })
                  console.log('error', error);
                });
            } else {
              let errorMessage = (typeof result.error === 'object' && Array.isArray(result.error.global)) ? result.error.global.join('\n') : null;
              if (errorMessage) {
                window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", errorMessage || "Something went wrong Try contact with us")
              }
              this.setState({ [type === 'invoice' ? 'isInvoiceMailSending' : 'isMailSending']: false })
            }
          }).catch(error => {
            this.setState({ [type === 'invoice' ? 'isInvoiceMailSending' : 'isMailSending']: false })
            console.log('error', error);
          });
      })
    }
  }
  getPostCodeAdresses() {
    const url = `${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/postcode-address`;
    let postCodes = [];
    //filtering
    [...this.state.reservation.selectedPickupPoints,
    ...this.state.reservation.selectedDropoffPoints,
    ].filter((item) => item.pcatId === 5 ? postCodes.push(item.postcode) : item);
    //configuration
    const config = { method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", }, body: JSON.stringify({ postcodes: postCodes, }), };

    fetch(url, config)
      .then((res) => res.json())
      .then((data) => {
        if (data.status) this.setState({ postCodeAddress: data.results });
      })
      .catch((error) => { console.log(error); });
  }
  checkPaymentStatus(paymentSessionData = {}) {
    let { reservation } = this.state
    let { webSocketToken, href } = paymentSessionData
    let interVal;
    if (webSocketToken) {
      interVal = setInterval(async () => {
        try {
          let req = await fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/payment/status`, { 'method': 'POST', 'headers': { "Content-Type": "application/json", }, 'body': JSON.stringify({ token: webSocketToken }) });
          let resp = await req.json();
          if (resp.status === 200) {
            //we r checking here in order to be sure it is stripe payment or not In future we can add more payments
            if (href.includes("stripe")) {
              window.manageBookingDispatch.setPaymentTokenAndEditReservation({ response: resp.data, reservation }, () => {
                this.setState({ cashCardPaymentDetails: null, isCashCardPaymentInProgress: false })
              })
            } else {
              window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Something went wrong Try contact with us")
              this.setState({ stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "" })
            }
            clearInterval(interVal);
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.log(error);
        }
      }, 2000);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Converts a given date-time string into different readable formats.
   * @param {string} dateTimeStr - A date-time string in "DD/MM/YYYY HH:MM" format.
   * @param {('short'|'full')} formatType - The desired output format.
   *    'short': returns "May 8" (default)
   *    'full': returns "08 May 2026"
   * @returns {string} The formatted date string.
   */
  formatBookingDate(dateTimeStr, formatType = 'short') {
    // Example dateTimeStr: "08/05/2026 18:35"

    // 1. Split the string into date and time parts
    const [datePart, timePart] = dateTimeStr.split(' ');

    // Extract day, month, year from the date part
    // Example: [ "08", "05", "2026" ]
    const [day, month, year] = datePart.split('/');

    // 2. Create a JS Date object 
    // NOTE: JavaScript Date uses 0-based month indexing → month - 1
    const dateObject = new Date(year, month - 1, day);

    // 3. Extract date components
    const dayOfMonth = dateObject.getDate();   // e.g., 8
    const fullYear = dateObject.getFullYear(); // e.g., 2026

    // 4. Get the English month abbreviation (e.g., Jan, Feb, May)
    const monthAbbreviation = dateObject.toLocaleString('en-US', {
      month: 'short'
    });

    // 5. Return output based on desired format
    if (formatType === 'full') {
      // Full format: "08 May 2026"
      // Ensure day is always 2 digits (e.g., 8 → 08)
      const paddedDay = String(dayOfMonth).padStart(2, '0');
      return `${paddedDay} ${monthAbbreviation} ${fullYear} ${timePart}`;
    } else {
      // Short format: "May 8"
      // (Better to append phrases like "Booked on" in the React component)
      return `${monthAbbreviation} ${dayOfMonth}`;
    }
  }


  // Output: "Booked on May 8"
  componentDidMount() {
    let { transferDetails: { transferDateTimeString } } = this.state.reservation
    this.getPostCodeAdresses()
    this.setState({ checkFor24: checkingHours(transferDateTimeString, { hours: 24 }), 'checkForZero': checkingHours(transferDateTimeString, { hours: 0 }) })
    window.reaervationDetailsDispatch = {
      setStripeIframeToNull: () => this.setState({ stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash: "" }),
      setSelectedPostCode: (results) => {
        let { postCodeAddress } = this.state
        let newpostcodeAdress = postCodeAddress;
        if (results.addresses.length > 0) {
          newpostcodeAdress.push(results)
          this.setState({ postCodeAddress: newpostcodeAdress })
        }
      },
    }
  }

  render() {
    let { isLuggageInfoOpen, payStripeLoadingInCaseCash, stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash, postCodeAddress, checkFor24, checkForZero, isMailSending, isInvoiceMailSending, isCashCardPaymentInProgress, isCashCardPaymentLoading, cashCardPaymentDetails } = this.state
    let { reservation, resources: { carsTypes, pointTypeCategories = [] }, eM, sM, reservationToken } = this.props;
    let carsTypesObject = Object.assign({}, ...carsTypes.map((obj) => ({ [obj.id]: obj })));
    let imageTypesObject = Object.assign({}, ...pointTypeCategories.map((obj) => ({ [obj.id]: obj.image })));
    window.pointsTypesCategories = Object.assign({}, ...pointTypeCategories.map((obj) => ({ [obj.id]: obj })));
    window.carsTypes = carsTypes;
    //for hansdle search adding item
    //=>flightDetails:flightNumber:""waitingPickupTime:0
    let objectDetailss = Object.assign(
      {},
      ...pointTypeCategories.map((obj) => ({
        [obj.id]: JSON.parse(obj.objectDetails),
      }))
    );
    let namePlaceTypesObject = Object.assign({}, ...pointTypeCategories.map((obj) => ({ [obj.id]: obj.categoryName })));
    //inside selected list Inorder to handle search mandatory or not
    let objectDetailStatuses = Object.assign(
      {},
      ...pointTypeCategories.map((obj) => ({
        [obj.id]: JSON.parse(obj.detailsStatus),
      }))
    );

    let {
      quotation,
      paymentDetails,
      transferDetails,
      passengerDetails,
      reservationDetails,
      selectedPickupPoints,
      selectedDropoffPoints,
      transferDetails: { specialRequests, transferDateTimeString }
    } = reservation;
    const formattedDateFull = this.formatBookingDate(transferDateTimeString, 'full');
    const formattedDateShort = this.formatBookingDate(transferDateTimeString);
    let hasCashCardPayment = (parseFloat(paymentDetails.byCash) && parseFloat(paymentDetails.byCash) > 0) && (parseFloat(paymentDetails.byCard) && parseFloat(paymentDetails.byCard) > 0)
    let totalPriceWithSymbol = `${(((__resources || {}).paymentCurrencies || {})[paymentDetails.currencyId] || {}).symbol || ' £'}${paymentDetails.price.toFixed(2)}`
    let { paymentType } = paymentDetails;
    let paymentTypeTitle = 'Paid By Card'; // 2,5,6,7
    if (paymentType === 1) { paymentTypeTitle = 'Pay Cash to Driver' }
    if (paymentType === 4) { paymentTypeTitle = 'Account' }
    if (paymentType === 5) { paymentTypeTitle = 'Paid By PayPal' }

    if (hasCashCardPayment) { // 3
      paymentTypeTitle = 'Cash/Card'
    }

    let detailsTabStatus = this.state.activeTab === 'details'
    let showEditableJourneyList = this.state.journeyEditStatus
    let showEditableContactInfoList = this.state.passengerEditStatus

    return (

      <div className="rsv-section">
        {showEditableJourneyList ? <React.Fragment></React.Fragment> :
          <div className="status-banner">
            {/* Left Section */}
            <div className="status-banner-ref-info">
              <p className="status-banner-label">Booking Ref</p>
              <h1 className="status-banner-ref-id">{this.props.reservation.reservationDetails.id}</h1>
            </div>

            {/* Right Section */}
            <div className="status-banner-status-container">
              <span className="status-badge">
                <img src={icons.checkCircle} alt="" />
                Confirmed
              </span>
              <p className="status-badge-date">Booked on {formattedDateShort}</p>
            </div>
          </div>}
        {showEditableJourneyList ? <React.Fragment></React.Fragment> :
          <div className="tab-switcher-container">
            <button onClick={() => this.setState({ activeTab: 'details' })} className={`tab-btn tab-btn-details ${this.state.activeTab === 'details' ? 'tab-btn-active' : ''}`} >
              <img src={icons.details} alt="" />
              Trip Details
            </button>
            <button onClick={() => this.setState({ activeTab: 'track' })} className={`tab-btn ${this.state.activeTab === 'track' ? 'tab-btn-active' : ''}`} >
              <img src={icons.track} alt="" />
              Track Driver
            </button>
          </div>
        }

        {this.state.setModalCar ? (
          <ModalInfo
            fromCar={true}
            setModalCarStatus={(e) => this.setState({ setModalCar: !this.state.setModalCar })}
            content="This is meant to give an approcimation of car size and category .Actual mane and model may vary"
          />) : ("")}
        {this.state.setModalFlight ? (
          <ModalInfo
            fromCar={false}
            setModalFlightStatus={(e) => this.setState({ setModalFlight: !this.state.setModalFlight })}
            content="Please note that on international flights, for UK and EU Citizens the average clearing time is around 45 to 60 minutes except for first & business class travellers where it is 30-45 minutes. Other nationalities take around 60-70 minutes and foreign students may take up to 90 minutes. For domestic flight, the clearance time is around 15 minutes"
          />) : ("")}

        {eM ? <AlertMessage eM={eM} /> : ""}
        {sM ? <AlertMessage sM={sM} /> : ""}

        {detailsTabStatus &&
          <div className={`rsv-section-container ${checkFor24 && reservationDetails.driverStatusId !== 9 ? 'rsv-section-container-with-alert' : ''}`}>

            {detailsTabStatus && showEditableJourneyList ?
              <JorneyDetailsUpdateForm
                reservation={reservation}
                quotation={quotation}//to quotationCardItem
                email={passengerDetails.email} //when he click to pay by card in case cash then we use it
                objectDetailss={objectDetailss}//to HandleSearch
                carsTypesObject={carsTypesObject} //to quotationCardItem
                postCodeAddress={postCodeAddress}//to SelectedList
                specialRequests={specialRequests}//to TextArea
                paymentToken={paymentDetails.token}//it is used whenever it is not cash payment (it is necessery in request body)
                imageTypesObject={imageTypesObject}//to SelectedList
                setModalCar={this.state.setModalCar}//state . to  quotationCardItem
                previousPrice={paymentDetails.price}//to inner     at the outset it is current previous When change quotation it will be previous one
                paymentType={paymentDetails.paymentType} //in order to make visible  py by card
                setModalFlight={this.state.setModalFlight}//state . to   selectedList=> CheckForFlight
                namePlaceTypesObject={namePlaceTypesObject}// to HandleSearch
                objectDetailStatuses={objectDetailStatuses}//to SelectedList
                selectedPickupPoints={selectedPickupPoints}//to SelectedList
                selectedDropoffPoints={selectedDropoffPoints}//to selectedList
                transferDateTimeString={transferDateTimeString} //to date input and to timepicker
                onSave={(e) => this.setState({ journeyEditStatus: false })}//to inner OnSave function of JorneyDetailsUpdateForm
                onCancel={(e) => this.setState({ journeyEditStatus: false })}//to inner onCancel function of JorneyDetailsUpdateForm
                setModalCarStatus={(e) =>
                  this.setState({ setModalCar: !this.state.setModalCar }) //to quotationCardItem
                }
                setModalFlightStatus={(e) =>
                  this.setState({ setModalFlight: !this.state.setModalFlight }) //to selectedList=> CheckForFlight
                }
              />
              :
              <JourneyDetailsDisplayedForm
                quotation={quotation}
                checkFor24={checkFor24}
                paymentDetails={paymentDetails}
                transferDetails={transferDetails}
                selectedPickupPoints={selectedPickupPoints}
                selectedDropoffPoints={selectedDropoffPoints}
                vehicleType={carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].name}
                onEdit={(e) => this.setState({ journeyEditStatus: true })}
                editDisabled={hasCashCardPayment}
                transferType={carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].transferType}
                isLuggageInfoOpen={isLuggageInfoOpen}
                formattedDateFull={formattedDateFull}
                totalPriceWithSymbol={totalPriceWithSymbol}
                reservationId={this.props.reservation.reservationDetails.id}
              />
            }
            {/* Vehicle & Passengers Grid */}
            <div className="booking-summary-details-grid">
              {showEditableContactInfoList && !showEditableJourneyList && (
                <PassengerDetailsUpdateForm
                  transferDetails={JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(reservation.transferDetails))}
                  maxPax={carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].pax}
                  passengerDetails={JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(reservation.passengerDetails))}
                  onSave={(e) => this.setState({ passengerEditStatus: false })}
                  onCancel={(e) => this.setState({ passengerEditStatus: false })}
                />
              )}
              <div className="details-card-grid-container">
                {/* Vehicle Card  This is visible on landing page Incase we edit customer details we need space to edit so that is why we dont show this section*/}
                {!showEditableContactInfoList && !showEditableJourneyList &&
                  <VehicleCard
                    carName={carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].name}
                    paxCount={carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].pax}
                    suitcaseCount={carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].suitcases}
                    carImage={`${__env.apiDomain}${carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].image}`}
                    luggageImage={carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].luggagesFiles[1]}
                    luggageImage2={carsTypesObject[quotation.carId].luggagesFiles[0]}
                  />}

                {!showEditableContactInfoList && !showEditableJourneyList && (
                  <PassengerDetailsForm
                    checkForZero={checkForZero}
                    transferDetails={transferDetails}
                    passengerDetails={passengerDetails}
                    reservationDetails={reservationDetails}
                    onEdit={(e) => this.setState({ passengerEditStatus: true })}
                  />
                )}


              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        }

        {/* opened iframe */}
        {(stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash || cashCardPaymentDetails) ? (
          <div className="iframe-rsv-container">
            <div className="iframe-div-in-case-cash">
              <div id='aplStripeElement' style={{ maxWidth: '500px', width: '100%', zIndex: 1000 }} data={JSON.stringify(stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash || cashCardPaymentDetails)}></div>
            </div>
          </div>) : ""}
        {!detailsTabStatus && <TaxiTrackerMap height="600px" reservationToken={reservationToken} />}
        <TransferAmendmentAlert checkFor24={checkFor24} reservationDetails={reservationDetails} />


        {/* here we control desktop payment blog */}
        {!showEditableJourneyList &&
          <div className="panel-container">
            {(hasCashCardPayment && isCashCardPaymentInProgress === false && reservationDetails.driverStatusId !== 9)
              ? <button onClick={e => this.payCashCard()} className="button-base">{isCashCardPaymentLoading ? 'Loading ...' : 'Pay your Cash by Card'}</button>
              : <React.Fragment></React.Fragment>}
            <button onClick={isMailSending ? e => { } : (e) => this.sendBookingAsEmail({ type: 'details' })} className="button-base">{isMailSending ? 'Loading ...' : 'Send Invoice'}</button>
            <button onClick={isInvoiceMailSending ? e => { } : (e) => this.sendBookingAsEmail({ type: 'invoice' })} className="button-base">{isInvoiceMailSending ? 'Loading ...' : 'Email Details'}</button>
            {/* if he  before paid with card Then it is not gonna be visible   */}
            {paymentDetails.paymentType !== 1 ? ("") : (
              (stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash || reservationDetails.driverStatusId === 9) ? "" :
                <button className="button-base pay-button" onClick={() => this.payByStripe(7)}>
                  <img src={icons.creditCard} alt="" />
                  {payStripeLoadingInCaseCash ? "Loading.." : `Pay ${totalPriceWithSymbol}`}
                </button>
            )}

            {paymentDetails.paymentType !== 1 &&

              <button className="button-base pay-button">
                <img src={icons.creditCard} alt="" />
                {`Paid ${totalPriceWithSymbol}`}
              </button>}
          </div>}
        {!showEditableJourneyList &&
          <FixedActionBar
            paymentDetails={paymentDetails}
            totalPriceWithSymbol={totalPriceWithSymbol}
            stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash={stripeIframeAndTokenInCaseCash}
            reservationDetails={reservationDetails}
            payStripeLoadingInCaseCash={payStripeLoadingInCaseCash}
            hasCashCardPayment={hasCashCardPayment}
            isCashCardPaymentInProgress={isCashCardPaymentInProgress}
            isCashCardPaymentLoading={isCashCardPaymentLoading}
            payByStripe={this.payByStripe}
            payCashCard={this.payCashCard}
            onTrackTaxiClick={() => this.setState({ activeTab: 'track' })}
          />
        }

      </div>
    );
  }
}

class TransferAmendmentAlert extends React.Component {
  render() {
    // Gerekli verileri props'tan alın
    const { checkFor24, reservationDetails, } = this.props;

    // Gösterim koşulu: (checkFor24 TRUE ve driverStatusId 9 DEĞİL)
    const shouldShowAlert = checkFor24 && reservationDetails.driverStatusId !== 9;

    if (!shouldShowAlert) {
      // Koşul sağlanmazsa hiçbir şey döndürme (sizin kodunuzdaki ": ("")" karşılığı)
      return <React.Fragment />;
    }

    // Telefon numarasını temizleme ve biçimlendirme
    const phoneNumber = String(__env.channelPhoneNumber);
    const cleanedPhoneNumber = phoneNumber.split(' ').join(''); // Tüm boşlukları kaldır

    return (
      <div className="alert-section-container">
        <div className={`alert_danger_check_for_24`}>
          You can only amend the transfer details up to 24 hours prior to
          your transfer time. Please call us on
          <a style={{ color: 'blue', textDecoration: 'underline', padding: '0px 5px' }} href={`tel:${cleanedPhoneNumber}`}   >
            {phoneNumber}
          </a>
          if you request any changes on your booking.{" "}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

"id": 10, "fieldType": "text", "fieldTitle": "description", "addressNeeded": "yes", "categoryName": "other", "image": "/media/qcushtroclifdnce3o0k.svg", "objectDetails": "{\"address-description\":\"\"}", "detailsStatus": "{\"address-description\": {\"pickup\": 2, \"dropoff\": 2, \"fieldType\": \"textarea\"}}" }], "paymentCurrencies": { "1": { "id": 1, "value": "EUR", "symbol": "Є" }, "2": { "id": 2, "value": "USD", "symbol": "$" }, "3": { "id": 3, "value": "GBP", "symbol": "£" }, "4": { "id": 4, "value": "TRY", "symbol": "₺" } } } || {},
      isAuth: false,
      showState: false,
      reservation: {},
      loginDetails: {},
      reservationToken: ""
    };
  }
  // Function to dynamically load the Zendesk script only when triggered
  loadZendeskScript = (callback) => {
    // Check if the script has already been added to the DOM
    if (document.getElementById('ze-snippet')) {
      console.log("Zendesk script is already loaded.");

      // IF ALREADY LOADED: Apply the settings to hide on close and hide initially.
      if (typeof window.zE !== 'undefined') {
        // 1. Hide the widget completely on the 'close' event (when the user clicks 'X')
        window.zE('webWidget:on', 'close', () => {
          window.zE('webWidget', 'hide');
        });
        // 2. Keep it hidden if already loaded (so the icon doesn't appear)
        window.zE('webWidget', 'hide');
      }

      // If loaded, execute the callback immediately
      if (callback) callback();
      return;
    }

    // Create the script element
    const script = document.createElement('script');
    script.id = 'ze-snippet';
    script.src = 'https://static.zdassets.com/ekr/snippet.js?key=473f7b02-4850-4045-8010-1fedf9752180';
    script.type = 'text/javascript';

    // Attach the onload event listener: call the callback when the script finishes loading
    // This ensures 'window.zE' is available when we try to open the widget.
    script.onload = () => {
      // WHEN SCRIPT IS LOADED: Apply the settings to hide on close and hide initially.
      if (typeof window.zE !== 'undefined') {
        // 1. Hide the widget completely on the 'close' event (when the user clicks 'X')
        window.zE('webWidget:on', 'close', () => {
          window.zE('webWidget', 'hide');
        });
        // 2. Keep it hidden after loading (so the icon doesn't appear initially).
        window.zE('webWidget', 'hide');
      }
      if (callback) callback();
    };

    // Append the script to the document body to initiate the download and execution
    document.body.appendChild(script);
    console.log("Zendesk script added to the DOM.");
  };

  // Function to open the Zendesk chat widget
  openZendeskWidget = (e) => {
    // Prevent default anchor link behavior
    if (e) e.preventDefault();

    // Check if the global Zendesk object (zE) is defined (meaning the script is loaded)
    if (typeof window.zE !== 'undefined') {
      // First, make the widget visible (override the hide command)
      window.zE('webWidget', 'show');
      // Then, open it
      window.zE('webWidget', 'open');
    } else {
      // If not loaded, initiate the script loading process
      console.log("Zendesk is not loaded. It will be loaded and opened now.");

      // Load the script and pass a callback function to run upon successful loading
      this.loadZendeskScript(() => {
        // Once the script is loaded, attempt to open the widget again
        if (typeof window.zE !== 'undefined') {
          // Since the script issues a hide command on load, show it before opening
          window.zE('webWidget', 'show');
          window.zE('webWidget', 'open');
        }
      });
    }
  };
  componentDidMount() {
    window.manageBookingDispatch = {
      onSuccessLogin: ({ 'data': reservation, reservationId, email, reservationToken }) => {
        this.setState({ reservation, 'isAuth': true, 'loginDetails': { reservationId, email }, reservationToken });
      },
      saveNewPassengerDetails: async (params = {}, callback = () => { }) => {
        let { passengerDetails, transferDetails } = params;
        let { language, 'user-id': userId, 'x-auth-token': xAuthToken } = this.props;
        let { reservation, loginDetails } = this.state;
        reservation.transferDetails = { ...reservation.transferDetails, ...transferDetails };
        reservation.passengerDetails = { ...reservation.passengerDetails, ...passengerDetails };
        loginDetails.email = reservation.passengerDetails.email;
        let fetchRes = await apiV1ReservationEdit({ reservation, loginDetails }, { language, 'user-id': userId, 'x-auth-token': xAuthToken })
        if (fetchRes.status === 200) {
          callback(fetchRes);
          this.setState({ "reservation": fetchRes.reservation, loginDetails })
          window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("Passenger Details Updated", "")
        } else { callback(fetchRes) }
      },
      saveStillWantsToDoesntChangePayment: async (params = {}, callback = () => { }) => {
        let { reservation } = params;
        let { language, 'user-id': userId, 'x-auth-token': xAuthToken } = this.props;
        let { loginDetails } = this.state;
        let fetchRes = await apiV1ReservationEdit({ reservation, loginDetails }, { language, 'user-id': userId, 'x-auth-token': xAuthToken })
        if (fetchRes.status === 200) {
          this.setState({ "reservation": fetchRes.reservation })
          callback(fetchRes);
          window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("Passenger Details Updated", "")
          this.setState(reservation)
        } else {
          callback(fetchRes);
          window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Something went wrong please contact with us")
        }

      },
      alertMessage: (sM, eM) => {
        this.setState({ sM, eM })
        setTimeout(() => { this.setState({ sM: "", eM: "" }) }, 4000);
      },
      setPaymentTokenAndEditReservation: async (params = {}, callback = () => { }) => {
        //this callback will trigger to changeeditstatus to true if payment happened successfully
        //when he/she is on the main page
        let { reservation, loginDetails } = this.state
        let { language, 'user-id': userId, 'x-auth-token': xAuthToken } = this.props;
        let { 'reservation': reservationOfPayment, response } = params;
        let { 'paymentTypeId': paymentType, token } = response
        reservation.quotation = reservationOfPayment.quotation
        reservation.selectedPickupPoints = reservationOfPayment.selectedPickupPoints
        reservation.selectedDropoffPoints = reservationOfPayment.selectedDropoffPoints
        reservation.paymentDetails = { ...reservationOfPayment.paymentDetails, paymentType, token }
        reservation.transferDetails = reservationOfPayment.transferDetails
        let fetchRes = await apiV1ReservationEdit({ reservation, loginDetails }, { language, 'user-id': userId, 'x-auth-token': xAuthToken })
        if (fetchRes.status === 200) {
          this.setState({ "reservation": fetchRes.reservation })
          callback(fetchRes)
          window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("Payment Updated Successfully", "")
        } else {
          callback(fetchRes);
          window.manageBookingDispatch.alertMessage("", "Something went wrong please contact with us")
        }
        window.reaervationDetailsDispatch.setStripeIframeToNull()
      },
      onCancelJourneyDetails: (reservation) => {
        this.setState({ reservation })
      },
      validatingTheReservationObject: (params = {}, callback = () => { }) => {
        let { reservation } = params;
        let { language, 'user-id': userId, 'x-auth-token': xAuthToken } = this.props;
        fetch(`${__env.apiDomain}/api/v1/reservation/edit`, {
          'method': 'POST',
          'headers': { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          'body': JSON.stringify({ 'reservation': [reservation], 'configurations': { onlyValidateReservationObject: true, checkReservationDetails: true }, language, 'user-id': userId, 'x-auth-token': xAuthToken })
        }).then(res => res.json()).then(resp => {
          callback({ ...resp })
        }).catch(error => callback({ 'status': 403, 'error': { 'global': [error.message] } }))
      }
    };
  }

class ManageBooking {
  constructor(elementId, options = {}) {
    this.elementId = elementId;
    this.options = typeof options === 'object' && !Array.isArray(options) && options !== null ? options : {};
    if (typeof window.React === 'object' && typeof window.ReactDOM === 'object') {
      if (this.options.mode === 'localhost') {
        console.log('check point 1 pass')
      }
    } else {
      throw new Error(`React or ReactDOM aren't exists`)
    }
  }
  render() {
    let demo = document.getElementById(this.elementId);
    if (demo && typeof window.React === 'object' && typeof window.ReactDOM === 'object') {
      ReactDOM.render(
        React.createElement(ManageBookingMain, { "user-id": __env.userId || 490, "x-auth-token": __env.xAuthToken || "24610b048c20464f0ca1aefbcab94c2c", ...this.options }),
        demo,
        () => this.onRender.bind(this)
      );
    } else { throw new Error(`there is no any Element has ID : ${this.elementId}`) }
  }
  onRender(callback) {
    if (typeof callback === 'function') {
      callback()
    }
  }
}
try {
  const __query = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
  const __demoId = __query.get('id') || 'manageBookingDemo'
  // const __manageBookingDemo = document.getElementById(__demoId || 'manageBookingDemo');
  setTimeout(() => {
    let manageBookingContainer = document.querySelector('.tool-manage-booking');
    if (!manageBookingContainer) {
      var manageBooking = new ManageBooking(__demoId, {})
      manageBooking.render();
      manageBooking.onRender(() => {
        console.log('rendered')
      })
    } else {
      console.log('is already mounted')
    }
  }, 1000);
} catch (error) {

}
